## CodeSystem: IMMZDAK CodeSystem for Decision Tables 

| | |
| :--- | :--- |
| *Official URL*:http://smart.who.int/immunizations/CodeSystem/IMMZDAK | *Version*:0.2.0 |
| Active as of 2025-11-25 | *Computable Name*:IMMZDAK |
